msg:I came to Liuzhou for a weekend trip. When I booked the room, I was reminded that there might be noise from the construction around. After checking in, I found that the store had prepared disposable earplugs at the bedside, and I was mentally prepared. Maybe it was because I checked in on the weekend? I found that there was no construction, and the environment of the hotel was really very quiet. The room is very large, and there is a tea table by the window where you can make tea yourself. The scenery outside the window is also very good. The toilet and bathroom are separated. What surprised me was that the hot water from the faucet was available immediately. It was probably zero cold water, which is better than many hotels of the same grade. You don‚Äôt have to wait for cold water when taking a shower. The afternoon tea is very exquisite, with two desserts, a bowl of sugar water and fruit drinks for self-service, which is different every day. The hotel is very close to the ancient town and the Industrial Museum, but there is no direct bus, and it takes about 20+ minutes to walk. Although the transportation is not particularly convenient, the taxi price in Liuzhou is cheap, and the average taxi is only about 10 yuan per time. The hotel also provides parking spaces for those who drive by themselves. Overall, the price is worthy of the environment, and it is also a very good weekend trip for me.
